        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there

get

        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





heap-use-after-free in the views::Widget::GetNativeTheme in the browser process  which will excape the sandbox.



<span class="line"><!---->heap-use-after-free in the views::Widget::GetNativeTheme in the browser process  which will excape the sandbox.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 95.0.4626.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 95.0.4626.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 && Ubuntu



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 &amp;&amp; Ubuntu<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





In the previous submission, it seems that the owner did not successfully reproduce in the initial report



<span class="line"><!---->In the previous submission, it seems that the owner did not successfully reproduce in the initial report<!----></span>



<br>





It can be reproduced stably in windows and linux.



<span class="line"><!---->It can be reproduced stably in windows and linux.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Steps:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Enable chrome://flags/#omnibox-webui-omnibox-popup



<span class="line"><!---->1. Enable chrome://flags/#omnibox-webui-omnibox-popup<!----></span>



<br>





2. open the chrome with the command : chrome.exe --user-data-dir=c:/tmp/any 



<span class="line"><!---->2. open the chrome with the command : chrome.exe --user-data-dir=c:/tmp/any <!----></span>





https://test.com/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://test.com/poc.html"><!---->https://test.com/poc.html<!----></a>





 about:blank



<span class="line"><!----> about:blank<!----></span>



<br>





3. input any strings in the omnibox 



<span class="line"><!---->3. input any strings in the omnibox <!----></span>



<br>





4. Mouse right click in the popup windows(chrome://omnibox/omnibox_popup.html)



<span class="line"><!---->4. Mouse right click in the popup windows(chrome://omnibox/omnibox_popup.html)<!----></span>



<br>





5. That will cause the UAF when the tab closes



<span class="line"><!---->5. That will cause the UAF when the tab closes<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





You can also reproduce this issue with the window.open api.



<span class="line"><!---->You can also reproduce this issue with the window.open api.<!----></span>

Some detail on what's going on here:



<span class="line"><!---->Some detail on what's going on here:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Menus have code to auto-close a menu if its parent widget loses activation.  In practice, this usually means that when a widget is closed, its open menu (if any) is closed too, because you can't generally open a menu on a widget without activating it in the process.



<span class="line"><!---->Menus have code to auto-close a menu if its parent widget loses activation.  In practice, this usually means that when a widget is closed, its open menu (if any) is closed too, because you can't generally open a menu on a widget without activating it in the process.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However, the omnibox dropdown doesn't activate when it opens, it leaves the parent widget active (with the omnibox textfield focused).  For normal Chrome builds this doesn't matter, because you can't context-click the omnibox dropdown (it doesn't do anything).  But the webui omnibox dropdown allowed a context menu to open.



<span class="line"><!---->However, the omnibox dropdown doesn't activate when it opens, it leaves the parent widget active (with the omnibox textfield focused).  For normal Chrome builds this doesn't matter, because you can't context-click the omnibox dropdown (it doesn't do anything).  But the webui omnibox dropdown allowed a context menu to open.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Combine these two together and you get an open menu that doesn't auto-close when its parent widget closes.  Somehow, this led to a UAF during menu painting; I'm not quite sure how, since I think that means the MenuHost widget was deleted but there was still a paint queued in the event loop, and I can't step through in a debugger because the code is now gone.



<span class="line"><!---->Combine these two together and you get an open menu that doesn't auto-close when its parent widget closes.  Somehow, this led to a UAF during menu painting; I'm not quite sure how, since I think that means the MenuHost widget was deleted but there was still a paint queued in the event loop, and I can't step through in a debugger because the code is now gone.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Maybe I'll try and resurrect this code just to debug more.



<span class="line"><!---->Maybe I'll try and resurrect this code just to debug more.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
